伊迪拉舰桥问答

返回舰桥问答目录

Psyker

条件选项

  • 显示条件：Quest；“伊迪拉，关于你的能力……”
  • 显示条件：Etude、Companion；“当时，阿洁塔看到那些破碎的透镜的时候，你的反应好像很激烈。”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“荒垄碑碣、N872-04号事故、技术枯萎病，你对这些词有印象吗？也许你的能力可以告诉你某些事情？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“你觉得我该送婕伊什么礼物？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“有什么新故事讲给我听吗，伊迪拉？”
  • 显示条件：有显示/选择条件；“你第一次穿越亚空间的故事还没讲完呢。”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“你很了解西奥多拉·冯·瓦兰修斯吗？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“那个假的西奥多拉伤害了你，你已经恢复过来了吗？”
  • 显示条件：Etude；“说真的，伊迪拉……人生很短暂。不如去找维格迪斯谈谈吧？她真的很担心你的情况。”
  • 显示条件：Companion；“你和阿洁塔之间的关系很紧张，对不对？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“关于这扇门，你的幻景有没有告诉你新的线索？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“伊迪拉，你还好吗？不后悔你当时的决定吧？”
  • 显示条件：Quest；“我听说，西奥多拉在达戈努斯和基亚瓦伽马星的某些地方留下了一部分藏匿处。你知道这件事情吗？”
  • 显示条件：Etude；“我想要你离开这艘船。”

选项索引

  • “伊迪拉，你还好吗？”
  • “咱们要怎么离开这个地方？你有什么想法吗？”
  • “你门后的那些朋友在说什么？有没有说什么有用的东西？”
  • “我得走了，要坚强。”
  • “伊迪拉，你还好吗？”
  • “咱们要怎么离开这个地方？你有什么想法吗？”
  • “你门后的那些朋友在说什么？有没有说什么有用的东西？”
  • “我得走了，要坚强。”
  • “伊迪拉，关于你的能力……”
  • “你是个灵能者，灵能者只有得到了帝皇的祝福，才拥有活下去的权利。你去过神圣泰拉吗？”
  • “我担心你可能控制不好自己的能力。”
  • “我很担心我的船员，与灵能者同行恐怕算不上太安全。”
  • “没什么。”
  • “当时，阿洁塔看到那些破碎的透镜的时候，你的反应好像很激烈。”
  • “这些话是什么意思？”
  • “或许我们应该警告阿洁塔？”
  • “你认为我应该盯着她吗？”
  • “荒垄碑碣、N872-04号事故、技术枯萎病，你对这些词有印象吗？也许你的能力可以告诉你某些事情？”
  • “你觉得我该送婕伊什么礼物？”
  • “有什么新故事讲给我听吗，伊迪拉？”
  • “你是从哪里来的？”
  • “你第一次穿越亚空间的故事还没讲完呢。”
  • “和我说说莱拉的情况吧。”
  • “上船之前你是做什么的？”
  • “你是怎么成为行商浪人的随行人员的？”
  • “你下过这艘船吗？”
  • “咱们来谈谈别的吧。”
  • “身为灵能者是怎样的感觉？”

  • “你能看到我的未来吗？”
  • “没问题！”
  • “还是下次再说吧。”

  • “你很了解西奥多拉·冯·瓦兰修斯吗？”
  • “那个假的西奥多拉伤害了你，你已经恢复过来了吗？”
  • “说真的，伊迪拉……人生很短暂。不如去找维格迪斯谈谈吧？她真的很担心你的情况。”
  • “做得好，伊迪拉。我们来祈祷最好的结果吧。”
  • “嗯，我们走着瞧吧。”
  • “你和阿洁塔之间的关系很紧张，对不对？”
  • “关于这扇门，你的幻景有没有告诉你新的线索？”
  • “伊迪拉，你还好吗？不后悔你当时的决定吧？”
  • “你现在说话的时候夹杂了太多的声音，哪个才是你自己的声音？”
  • “我始终愿意帮助你，伊迪拉。你的领主舰长绝不会把你引入歧途。”
  • “只要你还有用，我就不担心别的事情。”
  • “你看起来萎靡不振。情况很严重，很可疑。”
  • “非常好，这就是我的期望。”
  • “一个故事？那你可太低估自己了。咱们两个的冒险经历都足够写满一本书了！”
  • “并肩作战有点太近了，让人感觉不太舒服，毕竟你可能会再次失控。为了安全起见，保持手臂的距离似乎更合适。”

问答正文

伊迪拉来回踱着步，捂着耳朵，咒骂着某个看不见的人，偶尔陷入可怜的低语与啜泣中。她颤抖的手指仿佛有着自己的意志，不断地抠着异形装置留下的尚未愈合的伤口。
Idira paces back and forth, covering her ears, cursing at invisible interlocutors, and sometimes dissolving into pitiful whispers and sobs. Seemingly of their own volition, her trembling fingers pick at the unhealed wounds left by the xenodevice.

选项 Choices

  • 选择 Choice

“伊迪拉，你还好吗？”
"Idira, are you all right?"

伊迪拉哼了一声，仿佛你刚刚开了个好笑的玩笑一样。当她看到你还在等待她回答时，她直起了身子。“等等……你是认真的吗？老实说，舰长大人，我那群邻居们又从后门跑了进来，回到了我发了疯的小脑袋里。他们一定很想念我，因为他们比之前更吵闹了。但我猜，这总比变成异形手里的棋子，让他们在我身上做实验要好。”
Idira snorts as if you just made an excellent joke. When she sees that you are still waiting for an answer, she straightens. "Wait... you're serious? The thing is, Lord Captain, my neighbours from behind the door have come roaring back into my sick little mind. They must have missed me, 'cause they're noisier than ever now. But I guess that's better than being a pawn in the hands of xenos, doing experiments on myself."

“不好，我感觉好难受，难受得要死。那些声音又回来了，他们尝到了安静的滋味之后，变得比以往更加强烈，更加震耳欲聋。你当时要是把我丢在那里就好了，至少那样我可以平静地死去……”这个灵能者猛然意识到自己刚刚说了什么，她朝你投来了愧疚的目光。“请原谅我，舰长大人，我不是这个意思。我只是在呻吟，因为我感觉很难受。”
"No. I feel so sick I want to die. The voices are back, and after having that little taste of quiet, they seem more deafening and intense than ever. I wish you'd just left me there, at least then I would have died peacefully..." Realising what she just blurted out, the psyker shoots you a guilty look. "Forgive me, Lord Captain, I didn't mean that. I'm just moaning because I feel terrible."

  • 选择 Choice

“咱们要怎么离开这个地方？你有什么想法吗？”
"Any ideas on how we can get out of here?"

“好了，这么说吧，我们有一次去了落脚港……呃，我是说，西奥多拉领主舰长经常去落脚港，但有一次，出于某种原因，她把我也带上了。我那天过得很糟糕，早上一醒过来，脑子里就一直在嗡嗡响，但我也没别的办法，只能硬着头皮去。等我们到了那个地方之后，哎哟，那是个什么样的地方啊！所有的绅士与淑女都穿着光鲜亮丽的衣服，炫耀着他们镶嵌的植入物。所有人都簇拥在小桌子旁边……原来那是个赌场，而且并不是普通的赌场，而是某个腰缠万贯的人经营的赌场，有无数现金可以挥霍。你真应该看看当时的情形，那群人在一盘弑君棋上押上了好几颗行星！总之，领主舰长希望我能帮她打败某个人……于是我告诉她：‘那堆筹码你恐怕赢不到手’，‘你会拿到一手烂牌’，或是‘别坐在那张桌子旁边，夫人！’但她听吗？她当然不会听了。如果说有什么东西她从来都不缺，那就是她的固执。”
"Okay, so, we went to Footfall once... well, I mean, Lord Captain Theodora went to Footfall a lot, but on that occasion, she took me with her for some reason. My day had gotten off to a bad start, my head had been yammering since I woke up, but there was nothing else for it — I had to go. We arrive at the place — and what a place! All the gentlemen and ladies dressed to kill, showing off their encrusted implants, all clustered around little tables... Well, turned out it was a gaming den, and not just any gaming den, but one run by somebody with deep pockets for people with just as much cash to splash. You should have seen it — people gambling away planets in a game of regicide! Anyway, so the Lord Captain wanted me to help her beat some guy... So I tell her: the chips won't land in your favour, you'll get a bad hand, don't sit down at that table, Your Ladyship! But did she listen? Of course she didn't — if there's one thing she never lacked, it's stubbornness."

“于是他们就坐下来了，开始发牌。我当时在旁边晃荡，并没有参与那场游戏，但我一直在关注周围的事情，脑子里的声音也变得越来越响……总之，好在我及时意识到，我脑子里乱了套并不是因为我输了一手牌，而是因为别的什么原因。于是我便找了个借口，把领主舰长从桌子旁边拖走了，带她离开了那个地方。几分钟之后，就在那个房间里……”伊迪拉控制不住自己，突然大笑起来。“里面也有个聪明的家伙，也想到了同样聪明的打算。他也带着他的灵能者宠物一起去赌钱了！其中有个灵能者是生活在落脚港底层的那种，那个人……当场就吓坏了，我猜！他引起了骚动，之后所有人都去了那个房间，想看看到底发生了什么事情。随后，人们开始撕扯起了对方的喉咙！我是说真的！连牙都用上了！”伊迪拉擦了擦笑出来的眼泪。“嗯……后来，那颗小行星从落脚港彻底分离了出来。落脚港的人把它推到了空旷的宇宙中，让它朝着那个星系的恒星飞过去。”
"So, they sat down, and the cards were dealt. I'm hovering around, like I'm not involved, but I'm keeping my eye on things. And everything in my head keeps getting louder and louder... anyway, it's a good thing I realised in time that my mind wasn't going haywire over a losing hand, but something else. I made some excuse to drag the Lord Captain up from the table and took her away from that place, and a few minutes later, the room where we'd been..." Idira can't help herself and bursts out laughing. "It turned out some wise guy had the same bright idea to bring a pet psyker along with him! One of those ones who just scuttle around in Footfall's underbelly. And the psyker just... freaked out, I guess! After all the commotion, people went to see what happened in the room — and they'd all gone for each others' throats! Literally! With teeth!" Weeping, Idira wipes away a tear. "Huh... and I think they completely detached that asteroid from Footfall and pushed it off into open space so it would head off toward the local star."

Idira begins wringing her shaking hands. "I haven't been there in many years, but there's nothing for me to miss, trust me."

Like my first journey through the warp — I was in bed for three days, I felt like supernovas were exploding in my head! I only found out later that I'd gotten off easy — just through the bulkhead, in the bay next to mine, a whole team turned into—" Idira breaks off. "Look at me, rambling on, Lord Captain. Pay no attention."

Idira squints as though she's peering at something far away. "I can still remember the way the voices in my head changed when I looked at her — they were practically screaming. She had so much behind her... and plenty ahead of her, too."

“当我目不转睛地看着她时……我突然听到了一阵低语，一个暗示，一个建议，仅此而已，但我知道哪些话是闲聊，哪些话是真正的威胁。于是我抓住机会，靠近西奥多拉，想方设法在她耳边说了几句话，随后就被守卫拖走了。他们狠狠地揍了我一顿，把我关了起来。这也难怪，毕竟像我这样的人，是不允许与外来者交谈的……在那之后，西奥多拉的人就来找我了。他们轰塌了城墙，杀光了所有守卫，这样我才能把警告的全部内容完整地告诉他们。于是我说出了警告的剩余部分，但我不想再回到之前的生活，于是我便开始为冯·瓦兰修斯王朝效力。”

I seized my chance and approached Theodora. I managed to whisper a couple of words in her ear before the wardens dragged me away. They beat me and locked me up — no wonder, it wasn't my place to converse with outsiders... and then Theodora's people came for me. They broke down the wall, butchered the guards — all so I could tell them my warning in full. So, I said the rest, but I didn't want to go back to my old life — and so I entered the service of the von Valancius dynasty."

When I need to use it for work, I listen in more closely, but I usually just try not to notice it."

I swear on everything that's holy! I don't know what the second 'road' is or who watches over it, but, I beg you, stay away from it!"

“不要在坚固的地面上寻找，要去悬浮在虚空之中的金色大厅。在那里，有个没有亲族的孩子正在等待，她的名字不为人知。她握着画笔，在画布上涂抹着，但她却没有注意到，她的调色板上盛着的并不是颜料，而是鲜血。无论如何涂抹，那口井都不会枯竭，反而会不断填满，直到溢出……有一件事情确切无疑——当那口井溢出来的时候，没有人能逃过玷污。”
"Seek not on firm ground but in a golden hall suspended in the void. There waits a child without kin, but with a name blind to truth. She draws the brush across the canvas and does not notice that her palette is full not of paint but of blood. And with each smear, this well does not deplete, but fills, and fills, up to the brim... One thing is clear — when this vessel overflows, none will remain unstained."

“在无数盲目之人与假先知之中，某位红袍圣人正在寻求某个问题的答案。他不明白，他寻求的并不是答案，而是令一切成为焦点的问题。你会帮助他吗，行商浪人？但别忘了，有时无知比遗忘更加甜蜜。”
"Among the blind men and false prophets, a red-robed sage seeks the answer to a question. He does not know that it is not the answer he must seek, but the question that will draw everything into focus. Will you help him, Rogue Trader? But mark that sometimes ignorance is sweeter than oblivion."

“一条拴着链子的猎犬，追逐着极光散发出来的微光，但他的鼻子却被火花和汽油的味道迷惑。他身后拖着一条链子，如果你捡起了这条链子，会发生什么事情？你会成为他的主人/女主人吗？还是仅仅成为他真正主人手下的另一头猎犬？”
"A chained hound chases after glimmers of the aurora, but sparks and the scent of oil confound his nose. A chain trails after him — what will happen if you pick it up? Will you become his master/mistress, or merely another beast in the pack of his true lord?"

“黎明的光辉从监狱中迸发出来，地牢的高墙无法继续囚禁尘埃之中的黑暗之物。天真的小狗将它的鼻子伸向一只熟悉的手，而这只手在扭曲的玻璃之中，紧握着死亡。是要怜悯它的生命，还是要把它当做负担舍弃？变革之剑已高高举起，再多吞噬一个生命，又算得了什么呢？”
"The glow of dawn bursts forth from its prison — dungeon walls cannot contain the dark essence wallowing in the dust. A naive cub pushes his nose into a familiar hand, one that holds death in twisted glass. Cherish it or cast it off as a burden — the sword of change has already been raised, what is one more life to it?"

伊迪拉退了一步。她张开嘴，拼命地吸着气，仿佛有人刚刚一拳打在了她的肚子上。“黑暗悄悄地涌入我的喉咙，我的鼻孔。它在我的皮肤下蠕动，钻进了我的肺里，堵住了我的眼睛和耳朵，填满了绝望。我的周围，我的体内只剩下黑暗。”她突然停止了身子，大哭起来，困惑地看着周围。“请原谅我，舰长大人……这很古怪，但那些低语突然之间就沉默了下来。我不知道这意味着什么。我的直觉告诉我，这会是件可怕的事情。”
Idira flinches, her mouth desperately gulping down air as if someone just punched her in the gut. "Darkness creeps into my throat, my nostrils, it wriggles under my skin... It slips into my lungs and fills them with despair, blocking up my eyes and ears. There is only it, around me and inside me." She suddenly straightens and cries out, looking around in confusion. "Forgive me, Lord Captain... It's strange, but the whispers just fell silent all at once. I have no clue what it means. My intuition tells me it's something dire."

伊迪拉的声音铿锵有力，晶莹剔透，几乎带着戏剧性。“某个古老的世界中，有一颗裂开的心。找到通往它的道路，它的财富就属于你！但那里有两条道路，每条都会让你名誉扫地，而且每条道路都与看起来截然不同……你将如何选择，行商浪人？是选择至高天的罪恶，还是选择殒命诸神的罪恶？”
Idira's voice is sonorous and crystal-clear, almost theatrical. "An ancient world with a riven heart. Find the path to it — and its riches will be yours! But paths there are two, and both will cloak you in disgrace, and neither is what it seems... What will you choose, Rogue Trader? The fall of the Empyrean or the fall of the dead gods?"

“在你先祖的摇篮之中，有一头饥渴而狡猾的巨龙在吐着毒液。许多条道路从故乡延伸出来，但只有一条道路能返回故乡，一条充满悲伤的黑路。当你踏上这条路的时候，脚步要快！快点！再快点！”
"In the cradle of your ancestors, a black dragon hungers, cunning and spitting venom. Many paths lead from home, but only one leads back to it, black and full of sorrow. When you start along the path, make haste! Make haste!"

“一支自动羽毛笔煞费苦心地写着计划，一个字接着一个字地写着，一步又一步。然而，这张字条只会落得这样的命运——另一只手漫不经心地将墨水泼在它上面，用你的鲜血在别人的计划上写着。这只手由另一只手指挥，而另一只手又由另一只……那是谁的手？恐怖尖塔的阴影之中，是谁站在那里？”
"An autoquill painstakingly lays out the plan, letter by letter, step by step. But only one fate awaits this note — another's hand will carelessly douse it with ink, drawing over someone else's design with your blood. The hand is directed by another hand, and it, in turn, by another... Who? Who stands behind the shadows of monstrous spires?"

“帝皇石头的面孔是可怕的，但它却看不到祂脚下的烈焰。那个女人自称是祂的怒火，她的头顶戴着由星轨上的尸体组成的光环。然而，那些尸体燃烧时的样子并不相同，冷酷的算计甚至足以冲破正义的怒火。在你脚下，放着一个装满钷素的罐子。至于要把它倒在哪里，完全由你自己说了算。”
"The stone visage of the Emperor is fearsome, but it does not see the flames at His feet. The brow of the one who calls herself His retribution is crowned by an orbital halo of corpses. But they do not all burn the same — cold calculation can break even righteous anger. There is a canister of promethium at your feet, and where to pour it is your decision alone."

“在某个陌生世界的迷宫里，复仇的队伍正在游行，渴望以眼还眼。看到真相的人血溅四处，而那些遭到蒙蔽的人则会招致报复。在鲜血的吸引下，一头生病的野兽跑了过来，露齿狂啸。它的驯服仅仅是假象，它会将你带到十字路口。要么洗净毒血，欢声雷动，要么将大地染成一片血红。”
"In the labyrinth of a strange world, vengeance is served in procession: an eye for an eye. The spilt blood of those who see leads to revenge against those who were blinded. And drawn by the scent, a sickened beast comes running, baring its teeth. Its taming is a sham and leads to a crossroads — wash out the poisoned blood, revel in it, or soak the earth in scarlet."

“某件禁忌的遗物，发条制成的核心毫无节律地跳动着，每次跳动都会变得更加刺耳。与你同行之人，会为黎明让出道路。在铸造厂深处，一把充满毁灭之力的刀被锻造出来。这把刀你无法握住，一旦将它拔出，便会招致劫难与毁灭。”
"The clockwork heart of a forbidden relic beats out of rhythm, grating more with every throb. He who started on your path with you will make way for daybreak. In the foundry depths, a devastating blade is forged, one that you cannot hold. To unsheathe it is to call down doom and destruction."

伊迪拉的目光变得遥远，她的声音传来了不自然的金属回响。“在一切开始的地方，所有的道路重新交汇，一切都再次合而为一。踏入永恒之中吧，在那里，寂静的坟墓冒犯了心脏的搏动。这一步将会是最后一步。聆听你脑海中的低语吧，因为我的话语已经枯竭，行商浪人。”
Idira's gaze is distant and her voice multiplies in an unnatural metallic echo. "Where it all began and where the paths reconverged — everything has come together. A step into eternity, where the silence of graves offends the beating of hearts. This step will be the last. Listen to the whisper inside your head, for my words have run dry, Rogue Trader."

伊迪拉努力地倾听着，之后皱起了眉头，摇了摇头。“我很抱歉，舰长大人，这些声音开始发狂了，我什么都听不出来。我会想办法控制住它们，但现在的话……”伊迪拉为难地耸了耸肩，吸了吸鼻子。
Idira strains to listen, then frowns and shakes her head. "I'm sorry, Lord Captain, the voices are going wild — I can't make out a thing. I'll try to rein them in somehow, but for now..." The psyker shrugs sheepishly and sniffs.

伊迪拉努力地倾听着，之后皱起了眉头，摇了摇头。“我很抱歉，舰长大人，这些声音开始发狂了，我什么都听不出来。我会想办法控制住它们，但现在的话……”伊迪拉为难地耸了耸肩，吸了吸鼻子。
Idira strains to listen, then frowns and shakes her head. "I'm sorry, Lord Captain, the voices are going wild — I can't make out a thing. I'll try to rein them in somehow, but for now..." The psyker shrugs sheepishly and sniffs.

“还是下次再说吧。”
"Let's leave it for another time."

“行，没问题……只要你需要我，我就会在。”
"Sure, no problem... I'll be here whenever you need me."

“咱们来谈谈别的吧。”
"Let's talk about something else."

“没问题。”
"Sure thing."

伊迪拉侧过了头，仿佛在仔细听着什么。“很抱歉，舰长大人，但这就像是和天生目不视物的人谈论颜色一样。我可以花几个小时和你解释，但这对你而言毫无意义。”
Idira tilts her head to one side as though listening closely to something. "Lord Captain, forgive me, but it would be like talking to a person born blind about colours — I could spend hours explaining, but it wouldn't make any sense to you."

“每位灵能者都与亚空间有着独特的联系。有的人可以从眼角中看到亚空间的斑点与阴影，还有的人会感觉到亚空间的手指抚摸着他们的脊梁。至于我，我的脑子里有一扇门，只开了一条缝。无论我怎么努力，都关不上这扇门，我只能习惯来自另一边的低语。当我需要它为我服务时，我会更加仔细地去听，但绝大多数时间我都会试着忽视它。”
"Every psyker feels their connection with the warp in their own way. One person might see spots and shadows out of the corner of their eye. Another feels fingers running down their spine. As for me, I've got a door in my head, one that's open just a crack. There's no way to close it, no matter how hard I try — I've just had to get used to the whispers from the other side. When I need to use it for work, I listen in more closely, but I usually just try not to notice it."

  • 选择 Choice

“我想听听你的预言，伊迪拉。未来有什么样的景象在等待着我？”
"I'd like to hear your augury, Idira. What awaits me in the future?"

“没问题，咱们来听听他们有什么关于你的悄悄话，嗯？”伊迪拉笑了起来，搓了搓手，之后突然僵在了那里。她的脸上挂着空洞的微笑，头微微歪着。你感到皮肤上起了鸡皮疙瘩，衣领也开始微微颤动，仿佛某扇半开的门里吹来了微风。
"All right, let's hear what they're whispering about you, hmm?" Idira laughs, rubs her hands together — and suddenly freezes with a vacant smile on her face, her head slightly tilted. You feel goosebumps appear on your skin, and your collar begins to waver ever so slightly, as if moved by a breeze from a half-open door.

“是另一条路……这条路从扩区的门槛出发，延伸到世界的深……深……深处……”伊迪拉脸色发灰，大口大口地喘着粗气。另一个陌生的声音从她的喉咙中迸发出来，仿佛遥远的雪崩发出的沉重的轰隆声。“窥视命运之线并不是你该做的事情，王座上那具尸体的奴隶！踏入灾厄的怀抱吧，这就是命运的设计师为你设计好的命运！”
"Another road... the road begins at the threshold of the Expanse and leads to the bowels of the emerging wor... wor... world..." Idira turns grey and begins gasping for breath. A foreign voice tears its way out of her rasping throat — the deep, heavy rumbling of a distant avalanche. "Reading the threads of fate is not meant for you, slave of the enthroned corpse! Step into the embrace of doom, for thus was it preordained by the Architect of Fates!"

伊迪拉深吸了一口气，咳嗽了一声。某种蠕动的白色东西从她的嘴里飞出来，落在地上。那些白色的蛆虫一落在地上就立刻融化，变成了烟。“那……那不是我说的！我以所有的神圣之名发誓！我不知道那第二条‘路’是什么东西，也不知道是谁在看守它，但我求你，离它远点！”
Idira sucks in a breath and coughs. Something pale and wriggling flies out of her mouth and hits the floor — white maggots that immediately melt and turn to smoke. "I... that wasn't me! I swear on everything that's holy! I don't know what the second 'road' is or who watches over it, but, I beg you, stay away from it!"

“不要在坚固的地面上寻找，要去悬浮在虚空之中的金色大厅。在那里，有个没有亲族的孩子正在等待，她的名字不为人知。她握着画笔，在画布上涂抹着，但她却没有注意到，她的调色板上盛着的并不是颜料，而是鲜血。无论如何涂抹，那口井都不会枯竭，反而会不断填满，直到溢出……有一件事情确切无疑——当那口井溢出来的时候，没有人能逃过玷污。”

Idira strains to listen, then frowns and shakes her head. "I'm sorry, Lord Captain, the voices are going wild — I can't make out a thing. I'll try to rein them in somehow, but for now..." The psyker shrugs sheepishly and sniffs.

伊迪拉沉默了几秒钟，之后夸张地翻了个白眼。“你看……西奥多拉夫人才不在乎有没有哪个书呆子测量过我的大脑。你明白吗？重要的并不是你的脑门上有没有打过什么印章，重要的是你肚子里有什么，那些东西有没有烂。我的肚子比这艘船上的精金还要结实，而我的植入物比他们在泰拉的那些也要更好，不然我也活不到现在。”伊迪拉露出牙齿，露出了野性的笑容，眼中闪烁着热切的光芒。
Idira says nothing for a few seconds, and then exaggeratedly rolls her eyes. "Look... Lady Theodora couldn't care less if some eggheads measured my brains or not. It's not about the seal on your forehead, get it? It's about what's in your gut — if it's rotten or not. My gut's stronger than the adamantine on this here ship. And my implants are better than the ones they put in you on your Terra. If they weren't, I wouldn't have lived as long as I have." Idira bares her teeth in a savage grin, a febrile gleam in her eye.

"I mean, yeah, sometimes stuff happens... small stuff. Like when I hear things. Sometimes what I hear is so clear it becomes real to me. But even ordinary folks have bad days, don't they?"

“没问题，舰长大人。”
"Of course, Lord Captain."

伊迪拉空洞地看着你。“我想，说这些应该就够了，其他的事情并不重要。我是什么人，曾做过什么，这些都不重要。重要的是，我会忠实地为你服务，不会犯任何错误。”
Idira looks at you blankly. "I think that's enough. The rest doesn't matter. Who I was, what I did — it doesn't matter. What matters now is that I serve you — faithfully and with no mistakes."

  • 选择 Choice

“身为灵能者是怎样的感觉？”
"What's it like being a psyker?"

“很危险，充满危险。我很高兴我们找到了方法减轻这样的危险。为了我，为了你，也为了其他所有人。”
"Risky. Too risky. I'm glad we found a way to reduce that risk. For me, and for you. And for everybody else."

伊迪拉以嘲弄的眼神看着你。“不如你自己想想吧，舰长大人？”
Idira looks at you with derision. "You could ask yourself that question, eh, Lord Captain?"

“每位灵能者都与亚空间有着独特的联系。有的人可以从眼角中看到亚空间的斑点与阴影，还有的人会感觉到亚空间的手指抚摸着他们的脊梁。至于我，我的脑子里有一扇门，只开了一条缝。无论我怎么努力，都关不上这扇门，我只能习惯来自另一边的低语。当我需要它为我服务时，我会更加仔细地去听，但绝大多数时间我都会试着忽视它。”
"Every psyker feels their connection with the warp in their own way. One person might see spots and shadows out of the corner of their eye. Another feels fingers running down their spine. As for me, I've got a door in my head, one that's open just a crack. There's no way to close it, no matter how hard I try — I've just had to get used to the whispers from the other side. When I need to use it for work, I listen in more closely, but I usually just try not to notice it."

“你是如何忍受这种……窃窃私语的？”
"How do you live with this... 'whispering' in your head?"

“通过训练和习惯，一点点艾玛赛克酒，还有其他从下层甲板弄来的东西。只要把这些东西全都用上，就可以忍受得了那些声音。”伊迪拉耸了耸肩，笑着说。“有的时候我甚至怀疑，会不会大部分声音都是我自己想象出来的，尤其是船上的生活变得有点无聊的时候。不过，不管怎么说，这总比听活人说话要好。”
"Training. Habit. And a little amasec and a couple other things you can get on the lower decks. If you put all those together, it makes things bearable." Idira shrugs and chuckles. "Sometimes I even wonder if I'm imagining half the voices I hear. You know, when life on board gets a little boring. Better than listening to the living, anyhow."

  • 选择 Choice

“如果你那扇‘门’被冲开了，会发生什么事情？”
"What would happen if your 'door' burst open?"

伊迪拉试着露出笑容，但脸上闪过了一丝恐惧。“这么说吧……我想得越少，另一边的怪物就越不会感觉到我的恐惧。咱们还是别谈论这个话题了。”
Idira tries to smile, but fear darts across her face. "The thing is... the less I think about it, the less chance someone from the other side has to sense my fear. Let's not talk about it."

伊迪拉笑了起来，但她尖锐的笑声中充满了紧张。“这么说吧，如果门开了，就意味着有什么人打算闯进来，是吧？但去他的吧，我可不会让他们进来。相信我，我知道该如何紧紧锁住我宝贵的脑袋。”
Idira chuckles, but there is a shrill, strained quality to her laughter. "Well, if the door opens, that means somebody's planning to come in, right? But screw them, they're not coming through. Trust me, I know how to keep my valuable head locked up tight."

“你就不怕失去控制吗？”
"Aren't you afraid of losing control?"

Idira's eyes focus on you again. Her smile fades and her expression softens. "You know... what happened to me... well, you remember... I thought I'd go crazy with fear. But now that I know you've got my back, it's like that cursed whispering in my head has grown quieter. It's easier not to think about the worst that could happen."

“会失去控制的人，要么是惧怕自己能力的废物，要么是根本没搞清自己能力是什么的白痴，要么是总想瞎摆弄他们的新玩具的小屁孩。如果你不清楚自己能力的极限，或是总在你自己的脑子里瞎摆弄，那就一定会带来灾祸。”
"Only losers who are afraid of their own gift lose control. Or idiots who never figure out what they are before it's too late. Or little kids who want to play around with their shiny new toy. If you don't know the limits of your abilities or you're always bouncing around in your own head, that's a recipe for disaster."

So, I'm just going to... lean on that door in my head a little more, prick up my ears, and listen to what the warp's got to say about you." Idira grins like she's already heard some salacious detail. "If you'll allow it, I can listen right now?"

Step into the embrace of doom, for thus was it preordained by the Architect of Fates!"

伊迪拉深吸了一口气，咳嗽了一声。某种蠕动的白色东西从她的嘴里飞出来，落在地上。那些白色的蛆虫一落在地上就立刻融化，变成了烟。“那……那不是我说的！我以所有的神圣之名发誓！我不知道那第二条‘路’是什么东西，也不知道是谁在看守它，但我求你，离它远点！”

I swear on everything that's holy! I don't know what the second 'road' is or who watches over it, but, I beg you, stay away from it!"

“不要在坚固的地面上寻找，要去悬浮在虚空之中的金色大厅。在那里，有个没有亲族的孩子正在等待，她的名字不为人知。她握着画笔，在画布上涂抹着，但她却没有注意到，她的调色板上盛着的并不是颜料，而是鲜血。无论如何涂抹，那口井都不会枯竭，反而会不断填满，直到溢出……有一件事情确切无疑——当那口井溢出来的时候，没有人能逃过玷污。”
"Seek not on firm ground but in a golden hall suspended in the void. There waits a child without kin, but with a name blind to truth. She draws the brush across the canvas and does not notice that her palette is full not of paint but of blood. And with each smear, this well does not deplete, but fills, and fills, up to the brim... One thing is clear — when this vessel overflows, none will remain unstained."

"Among the blind men and false prophets, a red-robed sage seeks the answer to a question. He does not know that it is not the answer he must seek, but the question that will draw everything into focus. Will you help him, Rogue Trader? But mark that sometimes ignorance is sweeter than oblivion."

“一条拴着链子的猎犬，追逐着极光散发出来的微光，但他的鼻子却被火花和汽油的味道迷惑。他身后拖着一条链子，如果你捡起了这条链子，会发生什么事情？你会成为他的主人/女主人吗？还是仅仅成为他真正主人手下的另一头猎犬？”
"A chained hound chases after glimmers of the aurora, but sparks and the scent of oil confound his nose. A chain trails after him — what will happen if you pick it up? Will you become his master/mistress, or merely another beast in the pack of his true lord?"

“黎明的光辉从监狱中迸发出来，地牢的高墙无法继续囚禁尘埃之中的黑暗之物。天真的小狗将它的鼻子伸向一只熟悉的手，而这只手在扭曲的玻璃之中，紧握着死亡。是要怜悯它的生命，还是要把它当做负担舍弃？变革之剑已高高举起，再多吞噬一个生命，又算得了什么呢？”
"The glow of dawn bursts forth from its prison — dungeon walls cannot contain the dark essence wallowing in the dust. Cherish it or cast it off as a burden — the sword of change has already been raised, what is one more life to it?"

伊迪拉退了一步。她张开嘴，拼命地吸着气，仿佛有人刚刚一拳打在了她的肚子上。“黑暗悄悄地涌入我的喉咙，我的鼻孔。它在我的皮肤下蠕动，钻进了我的肺里，堵住了我的眼睛和耳朵，填满了绝望。我的周围，我的体内只剩下黑暗。”她突然停止了身子，大哭起来，困惑地看着周围。“请原谅我，舰长大人……这很古怪，但那些低语突然之间就沉默了下来。我不知道这意味着什么。我的直觉告诉我，这会是件可怕的事情。”
Idira flinches, her mouth desperately gulping down air as if someone just punched her in the gut. "Darkness creeps into my throat, my nostrils, it wriggles under my skin... It slips into my lungs and fills them with despair, blocking up my eyes and ears. There is only it, around me and inside me." She suddenly straightens and cries out, looking around in confusion. "Forgive me, Lord Captain... It's strange, but the whispers just fell silent all at once. I have no clue what it means. My intuition tells me it's something dire."

Idira's voice is sonorous and crystal-clear, almost theatrical. "An ancient world with a riven heart. Find the path to it — and its riches will be yours! But paths there are two, and both will cloak you in disgrace, and neither is what it seems... What will you choose, Rogue Trader? The fall of the Empyrean or the fall of the dead gods?"

“在你先祖的摇篮之中，有一头饥渴而狡猾的巨龙在吐着毒液。许多条道路从故乡延伸出来，但只有一条道路能返回故乡，一条充满悲伤的黑路。当你踏上这条路的时候，脚步要快！快点！再快点！”
"In the cradle of your ancestors, a black dragon hungers, cunning and spitting venom. Many paths lead from home, but only one leads back to it, black and full of sorrow. When you start along the path, make haste! Make haste!"

“一支自动羽毛笔煞费苦心地写着计划，一个字接着一个字地写着，一步又一步。然而，这张字条只会落得这样的命运——另一只手漫不经心地将墨水泼在它上面，用你的鲜血在别人的计划上写着。这只手由另一只手指挥，而另一只手又由另一只……那是谁的手？恐怖尖塔的阴影之中，是谁站在那里？”
"An autoquill painstakingly lays out the plan, letter by letter, step by step. But only one fate awaits this note — another's hand will carelessly douse it with ink, drawing over someone else's design with your blood. The hand is directed by another hand, and it, in turn, by another... Who? Who stands behind the shadows of monstrous spires?"

“帝皇石头的面孔是可怕的，但它却看不到祂脚下的烈焰。那个女人自称是祂的怒火，她的头顶戴着由星轨上的尸体组成的光环。然而，那些尸体燃烧时的样子并不相同，冷酷的算计甚至足以冲破正义的怒火。在你脚下，放着一个装满钷素的罐子。至于要把它倒在哪里，完全由你自己说了算。”
"The stone visage of the Emperor is fearsome, but it does not see the flames at His feet. The brow of the one who calls herself His retribution is crowned by an orbital halo of corpses. “在某个陌生世界的迷宫里，复仇的队伍正在游行，渴望以眼还眼。看到真相的人血溅四处，而那些遭到蒙蔽的人则会招致报复。在鲜血的吸引下，一头生病的野兽跑了过来，露齿狂啸。它的驯服仅仅是假象，它会将你带到十字路口。要么洗净毒血，欢声雷动，要么将大地染成一片血红。”

"The clockwork heart of a forbidden relic beats out of rhythm, grating more with every throb. He who started on your path with you will make way for daybreak. In the foundry depths, a devastating blade is forged, one that you cannot hold. To unsheathe it is to call down doom and destruction."

Idira strains to listen, then frowns and shakes her head. "I'm sorry, Lord Captain, the voices are going wild — I can't make out a thing. I'll try to rein them in somehow, but for now..." The psyker shrugs sheepishly and sniffs.

I swear on everything that's holy! I don't know what the second 'road' is or who watches over it, but, I beg you, stay away from it!"

“不要在坚固的地面上寻找，要去悬浮在虚空之中的金色大厅。在那里，有个没有亲族的孩子正在等待，她的名字不为人知。她握着画笔，在画布上涂抹着，但她却没有注意到，她的调色板上盛着的并不是颜料，而是鲜血。无论如何涂抹，那口井都不会枯竭，反而会不断填满，直到溢出……有一件事情确切无疑——当那口井溢出来的时候，没有人能逃过玷污。”
"Seek not on firm ground but in a golden hall suspended in the void. There waits a child without kin, but with a name blind to truth. She draws the brush across the canvas and does not notice that her palette is full not of paint but of blood. And with each smear, this well does not deplete, but fills, and fills, up to the brim... One thing is clear — when this vessel overflows, none will remain unstained."

“在无数盲目之人与假先知之中，某位红袍圣人正在寻求某个问题的答案。他不明白，他寻求的并不是答案，而是令一切成为焦点的问题。你会帮助他吗，行商浪人？但别忘了，有时无知比遗忘更加甜蜜。”
"Among the blind men and false prophets, a red-robed sage seeks the answer to a question. He does not know that it is not the answer he must seek, but the question that will draw everything into focus. Will you help him, Rogue Trader? But mark that sometimes ignorance is sweeter than oblivion."

“一条拴着链子的猎犬，追逐着极光散发出来的微光，但他的鼻子却被火花和汽油的味道迷惑。他身后拖着一条链子，如果你捡起了这条链子，会发生什么事情？你会成为他的主人/女主人吗？还是仅仅成为他真正主人手下的另一头猎犬？”
"A chained hound chases after glimmers of the aurora, but sparks and the scent of oil confound his nose. A chain trails after him — what will happen if you pick it up? Will you become his master/mistress, or merely another beast in the pack of his true lord?"

“黎明的光辉从监狱中迸发出来，地牢的高墙无法继续囚禁尘埃之中的黑暗之物。天真的小狗将它的鼻子伸向一只熟悉的手，而这只手在扭曲的玻璃之中，紧握着死亡。是要怜悯它的生命，还是要把它当做负担舍弃？变革之剑已高高举起，再多吞噬一个生命，又算得了什么呢？”
"The glow of dawn bursts forth from its prison — dungeon walls cannot contain the dark essence wallowing in the dust. A naive cub pushes his nose into a familiar hand, one that holds death in twisted glass. Cherish it or cast it off as a burden — the sword of change has already been raised, what is one more life to it?"

伊迪拉退了一步。她张开嘴，拼命地吸着气，仿佛有人刚刚一拳打在了她的肚子上。“黑暗悄悄地涌入我的喉咙，我的鼻孔。它在我的皮肤下蠕动，钻进了我的肺里，堵住了我的眼睛和耳朵，填满了绝望。我的周围，我的体内只剩下黑暗。”她突然停止了身子，大哭起来，困惑地看着周围。“请原谅我，舰长大人……这很古怪，但那些低语突然之间就沉默了下来。我不知道这意味着什么。我的直觉告诉我，这会是件可怕的事情。”
Idira flinches, her mouth desperately gulping down air as if someone just punched her in the gut. "Darkness creeps into my throat, my nostrils, it wriggles under my skin... It slips into my lungs and fills them with despair, blocking up my eyes and ears. There is only it, around me and inside me." She suddenly straightens and cries out, looking around in confusion. "Forgive me, Lord Captain... It's strange, but the whispers just fell silent all at once. I have no clue what it means. My intuition tells me it's something dire."

伊迪拉的声音铿锵有力，晶莹剔透，几乎带着戏剧性。“某个古老的世界中，有一颗裂开的心。找到通往它的道路，它的财富就属于你！但那里有两条道路，每条都会让你名誉扫地，而且每条道路都与看起来截然不同……你将如何选择，行商浪人？是选择至高天的罪恶，还是选择殒命诸神的罪恶？”
Idira's voice is sonorous and crystal-clear, almost theatrical. "An ancient world with a riven heart. Find the path to it — and its riches will be yours! But paths there are two, and both will cloak you in disgrace, and neither is what it seems... What will you choose, Rogue Trader? The fall of the Empyrean or the fall of the dead gods?"

“在你先祖的摇篮之中，有一头饥渴而狡猾的巨龙在吐着毒液。许多条道路从故乡延伸出来，但只有一条道路能返回故乡，一条充满悲伤的黑路。当你踏上这条路的时候，脚步要快！快点！再快点！”
"In the cradle of your ancestors, a black dragon hungers, cunning and spitting venom. Many paths lead from home, but only one leads back to it, black and full of sorrow. When you start along the path, make haste! Make haste!"

“一支自动羽毛笔煞费苦心地写着计划，一个字接着一个字地写着，一步又一步。然而，这张字条只会落得这样的命运——另一只手漫不经心地将墨水泼在它上面，用你的鲜血在别人的计划上写着。这只手由另一只手指挥，而另一只手又由另一只……那是谁的手？恐怖尖塔的阴影之中，是谁站在那里？”
"An autoquill painstakingly lays out the plan, letter by letter, step by step. But only one fate awaits this note — another's hand will carelessly douse it with ink, drawing over someone else's design with your blood. The hand is directed by another hand, and it, in turn, by another... Who? Who stands behind the shadows of monstrous spires?"

“帝皇石头的面孔是可怕的，但它却看不到祂脚下的烈焰。那个女人自称是祂的怒火，她的头顶戴着由星轨上的尸体组成的光环。然而，那些尸体燃烧时的样子并不相同，冷酷的算计甚至足以冲破正义的怒火。在你脚下，放着一个装满钷素的罐子。至于要把它倒在哪里，完全由你自己说了算。”
"The stone visage of the Emperor is fearsome, but it does not see the flames at His feet. The brow of the one who calls herself His retribution is crowned by an orbital halo of corpses. But they do not all burn the same — cold calculation can break even righteous anger. There is a canister of promethium at your feet, and where to pour it is your decision alone."

“在某个陌生世界的迷宫里，复仇的队伍正在游行，渴望以眼还眼。看到真相的人血溅四处，而那些遭到蒙蔽的人则会招致报复。在鲜血的吸引下，一头生病的野兽跑了过来，露齿狂啸。它的驯服仅仅是假象，它会将你带到十字路口。要么洗净毒血，欢声雷动，要么将大地染成一片血红。”
"In the labyrinth of a strange world, vengeance is served in procession: an eye for an eye. The spilt blood of those who see leads to revenge against those who were blinded. And drawn by the scent, a sickened beast comes running, baring its teeth. Its taming is a sham and leads to a crossroads — wash out the poisoned blood, revel in it, or soak the earth in scarlet."

“某件禁忌的遗物，发条制成的核心毫无节律地跳动着，每次跳动都会变得更加刺耳。与你同行之人，会为黎明让出道路。在铸造厂深处，一把充满毁灭之力的刀被锻造出来。这把刀你无法握住，一旦将它拔出，便会招致劫难与毁灭。”
"The clockwork heart of a forbidden relic beats out of rhythm, grating more with every throb. He who started on your path with you will make way for daybreak. In the foundry depths, a devastating blade is forged, one that you cannot hold. To unsheathe it is to call down doom and destruction."

伊迪拉的目光变得遥远，她的声音传来了不自然的金属回响。“在一切开始的地方，所有的道路重新交汇，一切都再次合而为一。踏入永恒之中吧，在那里，寂静的坟墓冒犯了心脏的搏动。这一步将会是最后一步。聆听你脑海中的低语吧，因为我的话语已经枯竭，行商浪人。”
Idira's gaze is distant and her voice multiplies in an unnatural metallic echo. "Where it all began and where the paths reconverged — everything has come together. A step into eternity, where the silence of graves offends the beating of hearts. This step will be the last. Listen to the whisper inside your head, for my words have run dry, Rogue Trader."

伊迪拉努力地倾听着，之后皱起了眉头，摇了摇头。“我很抱歉，舰长大人，这些声音开始发狂了，我什么都听不出来。我会想办法控制住它们，但现在的话……”伊迪拉为难地耸了耸肩，吸了吸鼻子。
Idira strains to listen, then frowns and shakes her head. "I'm sorry, Lord Captain, the voices are going wild — I can't make out a thing. I'll try to rein them in somehow, but for now..." The psyker shrugs sheepishly and sniffs.

伊迪拉努力地倾听着，之后皱起了眉头，摇了摇头。“我很抱歉，舰长大人，这些声音开始发狂了，我什么都听不出来。我会想办法控制住它们，但现在的话……”伊迪拉为难地耸了耸肩，吸了吸鼻子。
Idira strains to listen, then frowns and shakes her head. "I'm sorry, Lord Captain, the voices are going wild — I can't make out a thing. I'll try to rein them in somehow, but for now..." The psyker shrugs sheepishly and sniffs.

"Did you know Theodora von Valancius well?"

Idira shakes her head. "None of the officers knew the Lord Captain well. Not even Abelard, and she was always closer to him than anyone else. She told me from the off if I ever listened to anything in the warp about her without her permission, I'd be going out through the airlock. I'm not an idiot, so I never stuck my nose where it didn't belong — only when I was asked."

伊迪拉的眼睛变黑了，脸上浮现出古怪的表情，仿佛来自另一个世界。“我……我很难接受她已经离开的事实。冯·瓦兰修斯夫人给了我如今拥有的一切。是她让我看到了群星，带着我踏上了通往群星的道路。直到现在，我……我似乎依然能听到她的声音。”伊迪拉猛地吐了口气，摇了摇头。
Idira's eyes darken and a strange, otherworldly expression comes over her face. "It's... hard to wrap my head around the fact that she's gone. Lady von Valancius gave me everything I have. She opened the stars to me and the paths between them. I... I still think I can hear her voice." Idira lets out a sharp breath and shakes her head.

"Have you recovered from your encounter with the false Theodora?"

Idira nods solemnly, her eyes filled with a feverish gleam. "I have, Lord Captain! I remember our pact and I have myself under control. The voices haven't quietened... but I'm managing. And if I'm ever tempted to slack off..." She looks over her shoulder at her guard. "...I have a constant reminder of what's at stake."

Idira shakes her head. "No, Lord Captain, not a thing! And I'm wandering from bay to bay, scaring the crew. But don't worry — I'm sure that as soon as we get close... well, there'll be no mistaking it!"

You opened our— no, my! MY! Yes, you opened my eyes. I'm no longer scared of what's behind the door, because now I know for sure. I know nothing can threaten me when I'm with you. Thank you."

Idira smiles broadly. "Never been better, Lord Captain — no joke! As soon as I stopped fearing for my life, even the voices in my head quietened down. "Leira, an outlying world in the Heathen Stars region. In the Koronus Expanse, the deeper you go, the less visible the Astronomican gets and the less people know about the Imperium. The arrival of a Rogue Trader is the best thing that can happen to a world like that. The very best."

I only found out later that I'd gotten off easy — just through the bulkhead, in the bay next to mine, a whole team turned into—" Idira breaks off. "Look at me, rambling on, Lord Captain. “西奥多拉·冯·瓦兰修斯拜访了我当时侍奉的统治者。我不知道她找他有什么事情，反正也与我无关。”伊迪拉眯起眼睛，仿佛在窥视着远方的什么东西。“我依然记得，当我看着她的时候，我脑子中的声音发生了变化。那些声音几乎尖叫了起来。她身后有那么多东西……前面也有很多。”

She had so much behind her... and plenty ahead of her, too."

“当我目不转睛地看着她时……我突然听到了一阵低语，一个暗示，一个建议，仅此而已，但我知道哪些话是闲聊，哪些话是真正的威胁。于是我抓住机会，靠近西奥多拉，想方设法在她耳边说了几句话，随后就被守卫拖走了。他们狠狠地揍了我一顿，把我关了起来。这也难怪，毕竟像我这样的人，是不允许与外来者交谈的……在那之后，西奥多拉的人就来找我了。他们轰塌了城墙，杀光了所有守卫，这样我才能把警告的全部内容完整地告诉他们。于是我说出了警告的剩余部分，但我不想再回到之前的生活，于是我便开始为冯·瓦兰修斯王朝效力。”
"And as I gawped at her... all of a sudden I heard a whisper. A hint, a suggestion, nothing more. But I know the difference between idle chatter and a real threat. They beat me and locked me up — no wonder, it wasn't my place to converse with outsiders... and then Theodora's people came for me. They broke down the wall, butchered the guards — all so I could tell them my warning in full. So, I said the rest, but I didn't want to go back to my old life — and so I entered the service of the von Valancius dynasty."

When I need to use it for work, I listen in more closely, but I usually just try not to notice it."

I swear on everything that's holy! I don't know what the second 'road' is or who watches over it, but, I beg you, stay away from it!"

“不要在坚固的地面上寻找，要去悬浮在虚空之中的金色大厅。在那里，有个没有亲族的孩子正在等待，她的名字不为人知。她握着画笔，在画布上涂抹着，但她却没有注意到，她的调色板上盛着的并不是颜料，而是鲜血。无论如何涂抹，那口井都不会枯竭，反而会不断填满，直到溢出……有一件事情确切无疑——当那口井溢出来的时候，没有人能逃过玷污。”
"Seek not on firm ground but in a golden hall suspended in the void. There waits a child without kin, but with a name blind to truth. She draws the brush across the canvas and does not notice that her palette is full not of paint but of blood. And with each smear, this well does not deplete, but fills, and fills, up to the brim... One thing is clear — when this vessel overflows, none will remain unstained."

“在无数盲目之人与假先知之中，某位红袍圣人正在寻求某个问题的答案。他不明白，他寻求的并不是答案，而是令一切成为焦点的问题。你会帮助他吗，行商浪人？但别忘了，有时无知比遗忘更加甜蜜。”
"Among the blind men and false prophets, a red-robed sage seeks the answer to a question. He does not know that it is not the answer he must seek, but the question that will draw everything into focus. Will you help him, Rogue Trader? But mark that sometimes ignorance is sweeter than oblivion."

“一条拴着链子的猎犬，追逐着极光散发出来的微光，但他的鼻子却被火花和汽油的味道迷惑。他身后拖着一条链子，如果你捡起了这条链子，会发生什么事情？你会成为他的主人/女主人吗？还是仅仅成为他真正主人手下的另一头猎犬？”
"A chained hound chases after glimmers of the aurora, but sparks and the scent of oil confound his nose. A chain trails after him — what will happen if you pick it up? Will you become his master/mistress, or merely another beast in the pack of his true lord?"

“黎明的光辉从监狱中迸发出来，地牢的高墙无法继续囚禁尘埃之中的黑暗之物。天真的小狗将它的鼻子伸向一只熟悉的手，而这只手在扭曲的玻璃之中，紧握着死亡。是要怜悯它的生命，还是要把它当做负担舍弃？变革之剑已高高举起，再多吞噬一个生命，又算得了什么呢？”
"The glow of dawn bursts forth from its prison — dungeon walls cannot contain the dark essence wallowing in the dust. A naive cub pushes his nose into a familiar hand, one that holds death in twisted glass. Cherish it or cast it off as a burden — the sword of change has already been raised, what is one more life to it?"

伊迪拉退了一步。她张开嘴，拼命地吸着气，仿佛有人刚刚一拳打在了她的肚子上。“黑暗悄悄地涌入我的喉咙，我的鼻孔。它在我的皮肤下蠕动，钻进了我的肺里，堵住了我的眼睛和耳朵，填满了绝望。我的周围，我的体内只剩下黑暗。”她突然停止了身子，大哭起来，困惑地看着周围。“请原谅我，舰长大人……这很古怪，但那些低语突然之间就沉默了下来。我不知道这意味着什么。我的直觉告诉我，这会是件可怕的事情。”
Idira flinches, her mouth desperately gulping down air as if someone just punched her in the gut. "Darkness creeps into my throat, my nostrils, it wriggles under my skin... It slips into my lungs and fills them with despair, blocking up my eyes and ears. There is only it, around me and inside me." She suddenly straightens and cries out, looking around in confusion. "Forgive me, Lord Captain... It's strange, but the whispers just fell silent all at once. I have no clue what it means. My intuition tells me it's something dire."

伊迪拉的声音铿锵有力，晶莹剔透，几乎带着戏剧性。“某个古老的世界中，有一颗裂开的心。找到通往它的道路，它的财富就属于你！但那里有两条道路，每条都会让你名誉扫地，而且每条道路都与看起来截然不同……你将如何选择，行商浪人？是选择至高天的罪恶，还是选择殒命诸神的罪恶？”
Idira's voice is sonorous and crystal-clear, almost theatrical. "An ancient world with a riven heart. Find the path to it — and its riches will be yours! But paths there are two, and both will cloak you in disgrace, and neither is what it seems... What will you choose, Rogue Trader? The fall of the Empyrean or the fall of the dead gods?"

“在你先祖的摇篮之中，有一头饥渴而狡猾的巨龙在吐着毒液。许多条道路从故乡延伸出来，但只有一条道路能返回故乡，一条充满悲伤的黑路。当你踏上这条路的时候，脚步要快！快点！再快点！”
"In the cradle of your ancestors, a black dragon hungers, cunning and spitting venom. Many paths lead from home, but only one leads back to it, black and full of sorrow. When you start along the path, make haste! Make haste!"

“一支自动羽毛笔煞费苦心地写着计划，一个字接着一个字地写着，一步又一步。然而，这张字条只会落得这样的命运——另一只手漫不经心地将墨水泼在它上面，用你的鲜血在别人的计划上写着。这只手由另一只手指挥，而另一只手又由另一只……那是谁的手？恐怖尖塔的阴影之中，是谁站在那里？”
"An autoquill painstakingly lays out the plan, letter by letter, step by step. But only one fate awaits this note — another's hand will carelessly douse it with ink, drawing over someone else's design with your blood. The hand is directed by another hand, and it, in turn, by another... Who? Who stands behind the shadows of monstrous spires?"

“帝皇石头的面孔是可怕的，但它却看不到祂脚下的烈焰。那个女人自称是祂的怒火，她的头顶戴着由星轨上的尸体组成的光环。然而，那些尸体燃烧时的样子并不相同，冷酷的算计甚至足以冲破正义的怒火。在你脚下，放着一个装满钷素的罐子。至于要把它倒在哪里，完全由你自己说了算。”
"The stone visage of the Emperor is fearsome, but it does not see the flames at His feet. The brow of the one who calls herself His retribution is crowned by an orbital halo of corpses. But they do not all burn the same — cold calculation can break even righteous anger. There is a canister of promethium at your feet, and where to pour it is your decision alone."

“在某个陌生世界的迷宫里，复仇的队伍正在游行，渴望以眼还眼。看到真相的人血溅四处，而那些遭到蒙蔽的人则会招致报复。在鲜血的吸引下，一头生病的野兽跑了过来，露齿狂啸。它的驯服仅仅是假象，它会将你带到十字路口。要么洗净毒血，欢声雷动，要么将大地染成一片血红。”
"In the labyrinth of a strange world, vengeance is served in procession: an eye for an eye. The spilt blood of those who see leads to revenge against those who were blinded. And drawn by the scent, a sickened beast comes running, baring its teeth. Its taming is a sham and leads to a crossroads — wash out the poisoned blood, revel in it, or soak the earth in scarlet."

“某件禁忌的遗物，发条制成的核心毫无节律地跳动着，每次跳动都会变得更加刺耳。与你同行之人，会为黎明让出道路。在铸造厂深处，一把充满毁灭之力的刀被锻造出来。这把刀你无法握住，一旦将它拔出，便会招致劫难与毁灭。”
"The clockwork heart of a forbidden relic beats out of rhythm, grating more with every throb. He who started on your path with you will make way for daybreak. In the foundry depths, a devastating blade is forged, one that you cannot hold. To unsheathe it is to call down doom and destruction."

伊迪拉的目光变得遥远，她的声音传来了不自然的金属回响。“在一切开始的地方，所有的道路重新交汇，一切都再次合而为一。踏入永恒之中吧，在那里，寂静的坟墓冒犯了心脏的搏动。这一步将会是最后一步。聆听你脑海中的低语吧，因为我的话语已经枯竭，行商浪人。”
Idira's gaze is distant and her voice multiplies in an unnatural metallic echo. "Where it all began and where the paths reconverged — everything has come together. A step into eternity, where the silence of graves offends the beating of hearts. This step will be the last. Listen to the whisper inside your head, for my words have run dry, Rogue Trader."

伊迪拉努力地倾听着，之后皱起了眉头，摇了摇头。“我很抱歉，舰长大人，这些声音开始发狂了，我什么都听不出来。我会想办法控制住它们，但现在的话……”伊迪拉为难地耸了耸肩，吸了吸鼻子。
Idira strains to listen, then frowns and shakes her head. "I'm sorry, Lord Captain, the voices are going wild — I can't make out a thing. I'll try to rein them in somehow, but for now..." The psyker shrugs sheepishly and sniffs.

伊迪拉努力地倾听着，之后皱起了眉头，摇了摇头。“我很抱歉，舰长大人，这些声音开始发狂了，我什么都听不出来。我会想办法控制住它们，但现在的话……”伊迪拉为难地耸了耸肩，吸了吸鼻子。
Idira strains to listen, then frowns and shakes her head. "I'm sorry, Lord Captain, the voices are going wild — I can't make out a thing. I'll try to rein them in somehow, but for now..." The psyker shrugs sheepishly and sniffs.

"Let's leave it for another time."

"Sure, no problem... I'll be here whenever you need me."

“咱们来谈谈别的吧。”
"Let's talk about something else."

“没问题。”
"Sure thing."

伊迪拉侧过了头，仿佛在仔细听着什么。“很抱歉，舰长大人，但这就像是和天生目不视物的人谈论颜色一样。我可以花几个小时和你解释，但这对你而言毫无意义。”
Idira tilts her head to one side as though listening closely to something. "Lord Captain, forgive me, but it would be like talking to a person born blind about colours — I could spend hours explaining, but it wouldn't make any sense to you."

“每位灵能者都与亚空间有着独特的联系。有的人可以从眼角中看到亚空间的斑点与阴影，还有的人会感觉到亚空间的手指抚摸着他们的脊梁。至于我，我的脑子里有一扇门，只开了一条缝。无论我怎么努力，都关不上这扇门，我只能习惯来自另一边的低语。当我需要它为我服务时，我会更加仔细地去听，但绝大多数时间我都会试着忽视它。”
"Every psyker feels their connection with the warp in their own way. One person might see spots and shadows out of the corner of their eye. Another feels fingers running down their spine. As for me, I've got a door in my head, one that's open just a crack. There's no way to close it, no matter how hard I try — I've just had to get used to the whispers from the other side. When I need to use it for work, I listen in more closely, but I usually just try not to notice it."

“我想听听你的预言，伊迪拉。未来有什么样的景象在等待着我？”
"I'd like to hear your augury, Idira. What awaits me in the future?"

“没问题，咱们来听听他们有什么关于你的悄悄话，嗯？”伊迪拉笑了起来，搓了搓手，之后突然僵在了那里。她的脸上挂着空洞的微笑，头微微歪着。你感到皮肤上起了鸡皮疙瘩，衣领也开始微微颤动，仿佛某扇半开的门里吹来了微风。
"All right, let's hear what they're whispering about you, hmm?" Idira laughs, rubs her hands together — and suddenly freezes with a vacant smile on her face, her head slightly tilted. You feel goosebumps appear on your skin, and your collar begins to waver ever so slightly, as if moved by a breeze from a half-open door.

“是另一条路……这条路从扩区的门槛出发，延伸到世界的深……深……深处……”伊迪拉脸色发灰，大口大口地喘着粗气。另一个陌生的声音从她的喉咙中迸发出来，仿佛遥远的雪崩发出的沉重的轰隆声。“窥视命运之线并不是你该做的事情，王座上那具尸体的奴隶！踏入灾厄的怀抱吧，这就是命运的设计师为你设计好的命运！”
"Another road... the road begins at the threshold of the Expanse and leads to the bowels of the emerging wor... wor... world..." Idira turns grey and begins gasping for breath. A foreign voice tears its way out of her rasping throat — the deep, heavy rumbling of a distant avalanche. "Reading the threads of fate is not meant for you, slave of the enthroned corpse! Step into the embrace of doom, for thus was it preordained by the Architect of Fates!"

伊迪拉深吸了一口气，咳嗽了一声。某种蠕动的白色东西从她的嘴里飞出来，落在地上。那些白色的蛆虫一落在地上就立刻融化，变成了烟。“那……那不是我说的！我以所有的神圣之名发誓！我不知道那第二条‘路’是什么东西，也不知道是谁在看守它，但我求你，离它远点！”
Idira sucks in a breath and coughs. Something pale and wriggling flies out of her mouth and hits the floor — white maggots that immediately melt and turn to smoke. "I... that wasn't me! I swear on everything that's holy! I don't know what the second 'road' is or who watches over it, but, I beg you, stay away from it!"

“不要在坚固的地面上寻找，要去悬浮在虚空之中的金色大厅。在那里，有个没有亲族的孩子正在等待，她的名字不为人知。她握着画笔，在画布上涂抹着，但她却没有注意到，她的调色板上盛着的并不是颜料，而是鲜血。无论如何涂抹，那口井都不会枯竭，反而会不断填满，直到溢出……有一件事情确切无疑——当那口井溢出来的时候，没有人能逃过玷污。”
"Seek not on firm ground but in a golden hall suspended in the void. There waits a child without kin, but with a name blind to truth. She draws the brush across the canvas and does not notice that her palette is full not of paint but of blood. And with each smear, this well does not deplete, but fills, and fills, up to the brim... One thing is clear — when this vessel overflows, none will remain unstained."

“在无数盲目之人与假先知之中，某位红袍圣人正在寻求某个问题的答案。他不明白，他寻求的并不是答案，而是令一切成为焦点的问题。你会帮助他吗，行商浪人？但别忘了，有时无知比遗忘更加甜蜜。”
"Among the blind men and false prophets, a red-robed sage seeks the answer to a question. He does not know that it is not the answer he must seek, but the question that will draw everything into focus. Will you help him, Rogue Trader? But mark that sometimes ignorance is sweeter than oblivion."

“一条拴着链子的猎犬，追逐着极光散发出来的微光，但他的鼻子却被火花和汽油的味道迷惑。他身后拖着一条链子，如果你捡起了这条链子，会发生什么事情？你会成为他的主人/女主人吗？还是仅仅成为他真正主人手下的另一头猎犬？”
"A chained hound chases after glimmers of the aurora, but sparks and the scent of oil confound his nose. A chain trails after him — what will happen if you pick it up? Will you become his master/mistress, or merely another beast in the pack of his true lord?"

“黎明的光辉从监狱中迸发出来，地牢的高墙无法继续囚禁尘埃之中的黑暗之物。天真的小狗将它的鼻子伸向一只熟悉的手，而这只手在扭曲的玻璃之中，紧握着死亡。是要怜悯它的生命，还是要把它当做负担舍弃？变革之剑已高高举起，再多吞噬一个生命，又算得了什么呢？”
"The glow of dawn bursts forth from its prison — dungeon walls cannot contain the dark essence wallowing in the dust. A naive cub pushes his nose into a familiar hand, one that holds death in twisted glass. Cherish it or cast it off as a burden — the sword of change has already been raised, what is one more life to it?"

伊迪拉退了一步。她张开嘴，拼命地吸着气，仿佛有人刚刚一拳打在了她的肚子上。“黑暗悄悄地涌入我的喉咙，我的鼻孔。它在我的皮肤下蠕动，钻进了我的肺里，堵住了我的眼睛和耳朵，填满了绝望。我的周围，我的体内只剩下黑暗。”她突然停止了身子，大哭起来，困惑地看着周围。“请原谅我，舰长大人……这很古怪，但那些低语突然之间就沉默了下来。我不知道这意味着什么。我的直觉告诉我，这会是件可怕的事情。”
Idira flinches, her mouth desperately gulping down air as if someone just punched her in the gut. "Darkness creeps into my throat, my nostrils, it wriggles under my skin... It slips into my lungs and fills them with despair, blocking up my eyes and ears. There is only it, around me and inside me." She suddenly straightens and cries out, looking around in confusion. "Forgive me, Lord Captain... It's strange, but the whispers just fell silent all at once. I have no clue what it means. My intuition tells me it's something dire."

伊迪拉的声音铿锵有力，晶莹剔透，几乎带着戏剧性。“某个古老的世界中，有一颗裂开的心。找到通往它的道路，它的财富就属于你！但那里有两条道路，每条都会让你名誉扫地，而且每条道路都与看起来截然不同……你将如何选择，行商浪人？是选择至高天的罪恶，还是选择殒命诸神的罪恶？”
Idira's voice is sonorous and crystal-clear, almost theatrical. "An ancient world with a riven heart. Find the path to it — and its riches will be yours! But paths there are two, and both will cloak you in disgrace, and neither is what it seems... What will you choose, Rogue Trader? The fall of the Empyrean or the fall of the dead gods?"

Idira's eyes darken and a strange, otherworldly expression comes over her face. "It's... hard to wrap my head around the fact that she's gone. Lady von Valancius gave me everything I have. She opened the stars to me and the paths between them. I... I still think I can hear her voice." Idira lets out a sharp breath and shakes her head.

"If I knew I would've told you. Hearing things clearly requires cooperation from the other person, you know, but that cobra just hisses and spits its venom at me. I don't trust her one bit..."

After all the commotion, people went to see what happened in the room — and they'd all gone for each others' throats! Literally! With teeth!" Weeping, Idira wipes away a tear. "Huh... and I think they completely detached that asteroid from Footfall and pushed it off into open space so it would head off toward the local star."

“会失去控制的人，要么是惧怕自己能力的废物，要么是根本没搞清自己能力是什么的白痴，要么是总想瞎摆弄他们的新玩具的小屁孩。如果你不清楚自己能力的极限，或是总在你自己的脑子里瞎摆弄，那就一定会带来灾祸。”
"Only losers who are afraid of their own gift lose control. Or idiots who never figure out what they are before it's too late. Or little kids who want to play around with their shiny new toy. If you don't know the limits of your abilities or you're always bouncing around in your own head, that's a recipe for disaster."

  • 选择 Choice

“你能看到我的未来吗？”
"Can you see my future?"

伊迪拉皱了皱鼻子，环顾四周。随后她擦擦手，摇了摇头，最后又点了点头。“没问题，毕竟我就是干这个的。所以，我只要……靠在脑子里的那扇门上，竖起耳朵，听听亚空间是怎么评价你的就好了。”伊迪拉咧嘴笑了起来，仿佛已经听到了某些暧昧的细节。“如果你愿意的话，我现在就可以听，好吗？”
Idira wrinkles her nose and looks around. Then she wipes her hands, gives her head a shake, and finally nods. "All right. That's what I'm here for, after all. So, I'm just going to... lean on that door in my head a little more, prick up my ears, and listen to what the warp's got to say about you." Idira grins like she's already heard some salacious detail. "If you'll allow it, I can listen right now?"

  • 选择 Choice

“没问题！”
"Sure!"

“没问题，咱们来听听他们有什么关于你的悄悄话，嗯？”伊迪拉笑了起来，搓了搓手，之后突然僵在了那里。她的脸上挂着空洞的微笑，头微微歪着。你感到皮肤上起了鸡皮疙瘩，衣领也开始微微颤动，仿佛某扇半开的门里吹来了微风。
"All right, let's hear what they're whispering about you, hmm?" Idira laughs, rubs her hands together — and suddenly freezes with a vacant smile on her face, her head slightly tilted. You feel goosebumps appear on your skin, and your collar begins to waver ever so slightly, as if moved by a breeze from a half-open door.

“是另一条路……这条路从扩区的门槛出发，延伸到世界的深……深……深处……”伊迪拉脸色发灰，大口大口地喘着粗气。另一个陌生的声音从她的喉咙中迸发出来，仿佛遥远的雪崩发出的沉重的轰隆声。“窥视命运之线并不是你该做的事情，王座上那具尸体的奴隶！踏入灾厄的怀抱吧，这就是命运的设计师为你设计好的命运！”
"Another road... the road begins at the threshold of the Expanse and leads to the bowels of the emerging wor... wor... world..." Idira turns grey and begins gasping for breath. A foreign voice tears its way out of her rasping throat — the deep, heavy rumbling of a distant avalanche. "Reading the threads of fate is not meant for you, slave of the enthroned corpse! Step into the embrace of doom, for thus was it preordained by the Architect of Fates!"

伊迪拉深吸了一口气，咳嗽了一声。某种蠕动的白色东西从她的嘴里飞出来，落在地上。那些白色的蛆虫一落在地上就立刻融化，变成了烟。“那……那不是我说的！我以所有的神圣之名发誓！我不知道那第二条‘路’是什么东西，也不知道是谁在看守它，但我求你，离它远点！”
Idira sucks in a breath and coughs. Something pale and wriggling flies out of her mouth and hits the floor — white maggots that immediately melt and turn to smoke. "I... that wasn't me! I swear on everything that's holy! I don't know what the second 'road' is or who watches over it, but, I beg you, stay away from it!"

“不要在坚固的地面上寻找，要去悬浮在虚空之中的金色大厅。在那里，有个没有亲族的孩子正在等待，她的名字不为人知。她握着画笔，在画布上涂抹着，但她却没有注意到，她的调色板上盛着的并不是颜料，而是鲜血。无论如何涂抹，那口井都不会枯竭，反而会不断填满，直到溢出……有一件事情确切无疑——当那口井溢出来的时候，没有人能逃过玷污。”
"Seek not on firm ground but in a golden hall suspended in the void. There waits a child without kin, but with a name blind to truth. She draws the brush across the canvas and does not notice that her palette is full not of paint but of blood. And with each smear, this well does not deplete, but fills, and fills, up to the brim... One thing is clear — when this vessel overflows, none will remain unstained."

“在无数盲目之人与假先知之中，某位红袍圣人正在寻求某个问题的答案。他不明白，他寻求的并不是答案，而是令一切成为焦点的问题。你会帮助他吗，行商浪人？但别忘了，有时无知比遗忘更加甜蜜。”
"Among the blind men and false prophets, a red-robed sage seeks the answer to a question. He does not know that it is not the answer he must seek, but the question that will draw everything into focus. Will you help him, Rogue Trader? But mark that sometimes ignorance is sweeter than oblivion."

“一条拴着链子的猎犬，追逐着极光散发出来的微光，但他的鼻子却被火花和汽油的味道迷惑。他身后拖着一条链子，如果你捡起了这条链子，会发生什么事情？你会成为他的主人/女主人吗？还是仅仅成为他真正主人手下的另一头猎犬？”
"A chained hound chases after glimmers of the aurora, but sparks and the scent of oil confound his nose. A chain trails after him — what will happen if you pick it up? Will you become his master/mistress, or merely another beast in the pack of his true lord?"

“黎明的光辉从监狱中迸发出来，地牢的高墙无法继续囚禁尘埃之中的黑暗之物。天真的小狗将它的鼻子伸向一只熟悉的手，而这只手在扭曲的玻璃之中，紧握着死亡。是要怜悯它的生命，还是要把它当做负担舍弃？变革之剑已高高举起，再多吞噬一个生命，又算得了什么呢？”
"The glow of dawn bursts forth from its prison — dungeon walls cannot contain the dark essence wallowing in the dust. A naive cub pushes his nose into a familiar hand, one that holds death in twisted glass. Cherish it or cast it off as a burden — the sword of change has already been raised, what is one more life to it?"

伊迪拉退了一步。她张开嘴，拼命地吸着气，仿佛有人刚刚一拳打在了她的肚子上。“黑暗悄悄地涌入我的喉咙，我的鼻孔。它在我的皮肤下蠕动，钻进了我的肺里，堵住了我的眼睛和耳朵，填满了绝望。我的周围，我的体内只剩下黑暗。”她突然停止了身子，大哭起来，困惑地看着周围。“请原谅我，舰长大人……这很古怪，但那些低语突然之间就沉默了下来。我不知道这意味着什么。我的直觉告诉我，这会是件可怕的事情。”
Idira flinches, her mouth desperately gulping down air as if someone just punched her in the gut. "Darkness creeps into my throat, my nostrils, it wriggles under my skin... It slips into my lungs and fills them with despair, blocking up my eyes and ears. There is only it, around me and inside me." She suddenly straightens and cries out, looking around in confusion. "Forgive me, Lord Captain... It's strange, but the whispers just fell silent all at once. I have no clue what it means. My intuition tells me it's something dire."

伊迪拉的声音铿锵有力，晶莹剔透，几乎带着戏剧性。“某个古老的世界中，有一颗裂开的心。找到通往它的道路，它的财富就属于你！但那里有两条道路，每条都会让你名誉扫地，而且每条道路都与看起来截然不同……你将如何选择，行商浪人？是选择至高天的罪恶，还是选择殒命诸神的罪恶？”
Idira's voice is sonorous and crystal-clear, almost theatrical. "An ancient world with a riven heart. Find the path to it — and its riches will be yours! But paths there are two, and both will cloak you in disgrace, and neither is what it seems... What will you choose, Rogue Trader? The fall of the Empyrean or the fall of the dead gods?"

“在你先祖的摇篮之中，有一头饥渴而狡猾的巨龙在吐着毒液。许多条道路从故乡延伸出来，但只有一条道路能返回故乡，一条充满悲伤的黑路。当你踏上这条路的时候，脚步要快！快点！再快点！”
"In the cradle of your ancestors, a black dragon hungers, cunning and spitting venom. Many paths lead from home, but only one leads back to it, black and full of sorrow. When you start along the path, make haste! Make haste!"

“一支自动羽毛笔煞费苦心地写着计划，一个字接着一个字地写着，一步又一步。然而，这张字条只会落得这样的命运——另一只手漫不经心地将墨水泼在它上面，用你的鲜血在别人的计划上写着。这只手由另一只手指挥，而另一只手又由另一只……那是谁的手？恐怖尖塔的阴影之中，是谁站在那里？”
"An autoquill painstakingly lays out the plan, letter by letter, step by step. But only one fate awaits this note — another's hand will carelessly douse it with ink, drawing over someone else's design with your blood. The hand is directed by another hand, and it, in turn, by another... Who? Who stands behind the shadows of monstrous spires?"

“帝皇石头的面孔是可怕的，但它却看不到祂脚下的烈焰。那个女人自称是祂的怒火，她的头顶戴着由星轨上的尸体组成的光环。然而，那些尸体燃烧时的样子并不相同，冷酷的算计甚至足以冲破正义的怒火。在你脚下，放着一个装满钷素的罐子。至于要把它倒在哪里，完全由你自己说了算。”
"The stone visage of the Emperor is fearsome, but it does not see the flames at His feet. The brow of the one who calls herself His retribution is crowned by an orbital halo of corpses. But they do not all burn the same — cold calculation can break even righteous anger. There is a canister of promethium at your feet, and where to pour it is your decision alone."

“在某个陌生世界的迷宫里，复仇的队伍正在游行，渴望以眼还眼。看到真相的人血溅四处，而那些遭到蒙蔽的人则会招致报复。在鲜血的吸引下，一头生病的野兽跑了过来，露齿狂啸。它的驯服仅仅是假象，它会将你带到十字路口。要么洗净毒血，欢声雷动，要么将大地染成一片血红。”
"In the labyrinth of a strange world, vengeance is served in procession: an eye for an eye. The spilt blood of those who see leads to revenge against those who were blinded. And drawn by the scent, a sickened beast comes running, baring its teeth. Its taming is a sham and leads to a crossroads — wash out the poisoned blood, revel in it, or soak the earth in scarlet."

“某件禁忌的遗物，发条制成的核心毫无节律地跳动着，每次跳动都会变得更加刺耳。与你同行之人，会为黎明让出道路。在铸造厂深处，一把充满毁灭之力的刀被锻造出来。这把刀你无法握住，一旦将它拔出，便会招致劫难与毁灭。”
"The clockwork heart of a forbidden relic beats out of rhythm, grating more with every throb. He who started on your path with you will make way for daybreak. In the foundry depths, a devastating blade is forged, one that you cannot hold. To unsheathe it is to call down doom and destruction."

伊迪拉的目光变得遥远，她的声音传来了不自然的金属回响。“在一切开始的地方，所有的道路重新交汇，一切都再次合而为一。踏入永恒之中吧，在那里，寂静的坟墓冒犯了心脏的搏动。这一步将会是最后一步。聆听你脑海中的低语吧，因为我的话语已经枯竭，行商浪人。”
Idira's gaze is distant and her voice multiplies in an unnatural metallic echo. "Where it all began and where the paths reconverged — everything has come together. A step into eternity, where the silence of graves offends the beating of hearts. This step will be the last. Listen to the whisper inside your head, for my words have run dry, Rogue Trader."

伊迪拉努力地倾听着，之后皱起了眉头，摇了摇头。“我很抱歉，舰长大人，这些声音开始发狂了，我什么都听不出来。我会想办法控制住它们，但现在的话……”伊迪拉为难地耸了耸肩，吸了吸鼻子。
Idira strains to listen, then frowns and shakes her head. "I'm sorry, Lord Captain, the voices are going wild — I can't make out a thing. I'll try to rein them in somehow, but for now..." The psyker shrugs sheepishly and sniffs.

伊迪拉努力地倾听着，之后皱起了眉头，摇了摇头。“我很抱歉，舰长大人，这些声音开始发狂了，我什么都听不出来。我会想办法控制住它们，但现在的话……”伊迪拉为难地耸了耸肩，吸了吸鼻子。

When I need to use it for work, I listen in more closely, but I usually just try not to notice it."

Idira's voice is sonorous and crystal-clear, almost theatrical. "An ancient world with a riven heart. Find the path to it — and its riches will be yours! But paths there are two, and both will cloak you in disgrace, and neither is what it seems... What will you choose, Rogue Trader? The fall of the Empyrean or the fall of the dead gods?"

“在你先祖的摇篮之中，有一头饥渴而狡猾的巨龙在吐着毒液。许多条道路从故乡延伸出来，但只有一条道路能返回故乡，一条充满悲伤的黑路。当你踏上这条路的时候，脚步要快！快点！再快点！”
"In the cradle of your ancestors, a black dragon hungers, cunning and spitting venom. Many paths lead from home, but only one leads back to it, black and full of sorrow. When you start along the path, make haste! Make haste!"

“一支自动羽毛笔煞费苦心地写着计划，一个字接着一个字地写着，一步又一步。然而，这张字条只会落得这样的命运——另一只手漫不经心地将墨水泼在它上面，用你的鲜血在别人的计划上写着。这只手由另一只手指挥，而另一只手又由另一只……那是谁的手？恐怖尖塔的阴影之中，是谁站在那里？”
"An autoquill painstakingly lays out the plan, letter by letter, step by step. But only one fate awaits this note — another's hand will carelessly douse it with ink, drawing over someone else's design with your blood. The hand is directed by another hand, and it, in turn, by another... Who? Who stands behind the shadows of monstrous spires?"

“帝皇石头的面孔是可怕的，但它却看不到祂脚下的烈焰。那个女人自称是祂的怒火，她的头顶戴着由星轨上的尸体组成的光环。然而，那些尸体燃烧时的样子并不相同，冷酷的算计甚至足以冲破正义的怒火。在你脚下，放着一个装满钷素的罐子。至于要把它倒在哪里，完全由你自己说了算。”
"The stone visage of the Emperor is fearsome, but it does not see the flames at His feet. The brow of the one who calls herself His retribution is crowned by an orbital halo of corpses. But they do not all burn the same — cold calculation can break even righteous anger. There is a canister of promethium at your feet, and where to pour it is your decision alone."

“在某个陌生世界的迷宫里，复仇的队伍正在游行，渴望以眼还眼。看到真相的人血溅四处，而那些遭到蒙蔽的人则会招致报复。在鲜血的吸引下，一头生病的野兽跑了过来，露齿狂啸。它的驯服仅仅是假象，它会将你带到十字路口。要么洗净毒血，欢声雷动，要么将大地染成一片血红。”
"In the labyrinth of a strange world, vengeance is served in procession: an eye for an eye. The spilt blood of those who see leads to revenge against those who were blinded. And drawn by the scent, a sickened beast comes running, baring its teeth. Its taming is a sham and leads to a crossroads — wash out the poisoned blood, revel in it, or soak the earth in scarlet."

“某件禁忌的遗物，发条制成的核心毫无节律地跳动着，每次跳动都会变得更加刺耳。与你同行之人，会为黎明让出道路。在铸造厂深处，一把充满毁灭之力的刀被锻造出来。这把刀你无法握住，一旦将它拔出，便会招致劫难与毁灭。”
"The clockwork heart of a forbidden relic beats out of rhythm, grating more with every throb. He who started on your path with you will make way for daybreak. In the foundry depths, a devastating blade is forged, one that you cannot hold. To unsheathe it is to call down doom and destruction."

伊迪拉的目光变得遥远，她的声音传来了不自然的金属回响。“在一切开始的地方，所有的道路重新交汇，一切都再次合而为一。踏入永恒之中吧，在那里，寂静的坟墓冒犯了心脏的搏动。这一步将会是最后一步。聆听你脑海中的低语吧，因为我的话语已经枯竭，行商浪人。”
Idira's gaze is distant and her voice multiplies in an unnatural metallic echo. "Where it all began and where the paths reconverged — everything has come together. A step into eternity, where the silence of graves offends the beating of hearts. This step will be the last. Listen to the whisper inside your head, for my words have run dry, Rogue Trader."

伊迪拉努力地倾听着，之后皱起了眉头，摇了摇头。“我很抱歉，舰长大人，这些声音开始发狂了，我什么都听不出来。我会想办法控制住它们，但现在的话……”伊迪拉为难地耸了耸肩，吸了吸鼻子。
Idira strains to listen, then frowns and shakes her head. "I'm sorry, Lord Captain, the voices are going wild — I can't make out a thing. I'll try to rein them in somehow, but for now..." The psyker shrugs sheepishly and sniffs.

伊迪拉努力地倾听着，之后皱起了眉头，摇了摇头。“我很抱歉，舰长大人，这些声音开始发狂了，我什么都听不出来。我会想办法控制住它们，但现在的话……”伊迪拉为难地耸了耸肩，吸了吸鼻子。

Idira's eyes darken and a strange, otherworldly expression comes over her face. "It's... hard to wrap my head around the fact that she's gone. Lady von Valancius gave me everything I have. She opened the stars to me and the paths between them. I... I still think I can hear her voice." Idira lets out a sharp breath and shakes her head.

And if I'm ever tempted to slack off..." She looks over her shoulder at her guard. "...I have a constant reminder of what's at stake."

I don't know who Lady Theodora would've told about a thing like that, but it definitely wasn't m—" She breaks off, appearing to listen to something. Grief passes over her face like a shadow. "Why would you whisper that to me now? Why?"

伊迪拉的声音颤抖而低沉。“舰长大人，我不知道什么藏匿处，也不知道西奥多拉夫人的秘密，但那些声音……那些声音在提醒我某件事。我曾经品尝过真正的美酒，是西奥多拉夫人给我的……那不是普通的合成酒，而是她最喜欢的那种烈酒，她以前经常在宫殿里喝。那种酒的颜色是金色的，名字叫‘纯净之火’。名字很蠢，但味道却很香醇。无论是在那之前还是之后，我都再也没喝过那么好的酒……”伊迪拉悲伤地抽着鼻子，然后摇摇头。“抱歉，这件事可能并不重要，但除此之外，别的事情我恐怕都不清楚。”
Idira speaks quietly, her voice trembling. "Lord Captain, I don't know anything about caches or Lady Theodora's secrets, but the voices... the voices have just reminded me about something. I was once given the chance to try some real wine — Lady Theodora gave me some... Not just any old synthetic booze, but her favourite plonk. She always drank it in her palace. It was golden in colour, and its name was Flame of Purity. A silly name, but the flavour was so intense and like nothing I'd ever tasted before or since..." Sniffing sadly, Idira shakes her head. "Apologies. It's probably not important, but I don't know anything more than that."

  • 选择 Choice

“我想要你离开这艘船。”
"I want you to leave the ship."

伊迪拉愣住了，她的眼神中渐渐地充满了恐惧。“什么？”
Idira freezes, her eyes beginning to fill with fear. "What?"

"I repeat: the next habitable world we come to, you're off my ship."

伊迪拉退了一步，仿佛被猛地击中了。“可这是为什么？”她盯着你的脸，似乎在你的表情中找到了答案。随后，她发出一声颤抖的叹息，点了点头。“遵、遵命，舰长大人。我会……开始收拾东西的，永别了。”
Idira steps back like she's been struck. "But why?" She stares at your face and seems to find an answer there, because she lets out a trembling sigh and nods. "Y-yes, Lord Captain. I'll... start making arrangements. Farewell."
